Line 4 THE COURT: Welcome back. I want to give you a
Line 5 couple more instructions before we invite the parties to make
Line 6 opening statements.
Line 7 As jurors, it is your responsibility to determine the
Line 8 credibility of each witness and the weight to be given the
Line 9 testimony of each witness. In order to make this
Line 10 determination, you may properly consider the overall reaction
Line 11 of the witness while testifying, his or her frankness or lack
Line 12 of frankness, his or her interest or bias, if any, the means
Line 13 and opportunity the witness had to know the facts about which
Line 14 he or she testifies, the reasonableness or unreasonableness of
Line 15 his or her testimony in light of all the evidence in the case.
Line 16 You’re not required to believe the testimony of any
Line 17 witness simply because he or she is under oath. You may
Line 18 believe or disbelieve all or part of the testimony of any
Line 19 witness. It’s your duty to determine what testimony is worthy
Line 20 of belief and what testimony is not worthy of belief.
Line 21 It’s my responsibility as the judge to ensure the
Line 22 evidence is presented according to the law, to instruct you as
Line 23 to the law, and to rule on objections raised by the attorneys.
Line 24 No statement or ruling by me is intended to indicate any
Line 25 opinion concerning the facts or the evidence.
